# Email Generation Prompts

All prompts used to generate the hero email for each campaign across all brands.

---

## 2 Dogs Treats
**URL:** https://www.2dogstreats.com  
**Vertical:** DTC Pet Food / Dog Treats  
**Summary:** 2 Dogs Treats is a Boston-based direct-to-consumer brand that makes single-ingredient, human-grade dog treats and chews in small batches (Just Chicken, Just Beef, fish skins, organic sweet potato, Summit chews), plus a Build-a-Box and gift boxes. It serves health-conscious dog owners who want full ingredient transparency, especially those whose dogs have allergies, sensitivities, or picky palates, and who will pay a premium for treats they can trust. Revenue is self-serve e-commerce with an available subscription, backed by a full satisfaction-guarantee refund.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Activate a new subscriber or first-time buyer by pre-framing the 'aha' moment (dog goes wild + owner flips the bag to one ingredient) and driving the first or second order.  
**Rationale:** There's no welcome flow today beyond a likely-thin Shopify default, and welcome emails are the most-opened a brand sends. This is the fastest way to set the single-ingredient philosophy and remove first-purchase hesitation with the satisfaction guarantee.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "2 Dogs Treats".

Brand colors: primary #1C4E7F, accent #D07832, background #FAFAF8, text #2C2C2C.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Welcome & Onboarding — Activate a new subscriber or first-time buyer by pre-framing the 'aha' moment (dog goes wild + owner flips the bag to one ingredient) and driving the first or second order.
- Subject: Welcome to the pack — flip the bag, every time
- Preview/preheader: One ingredient. That's the whole list. Here's why that matters for your pup.
- Purpose: Warm founder welcome, set the single-ingredient promise, and pre-frame the first-delivery 'aha' moment so the customer knows what to watch for.
- Primary CTA: Shop single-ingredient treats
- Key points: Founder-led hello from Mike & Riley's story; warm, neighbor-not-marketer tone | The promise: every bag is ONE ingredient — no fillers, preservatives, or mystery meat, made in our Boston kitchen | Pre-frame the aha: 'When your order lands, watch your pup's reaction, then flip the bag and read the whole ingredient list in two seconds' | Risk reversal: full refund if your dog doesn't love it — zero risk to try | Reply-to is a real person at woof@2dogstreats.com
```

### Campaign 2: Newsletter Subscriber to First Purchase
**Objective:** Convert engaged newsletter subscribers who haven't yet bought into a first order, using the satisfaction guarantee as the brand's trial substitute.  
**Rationale:** Newsletter-to-first-purchase is a named primary goal and the core revenue play; with no free trial, the deciding email must neutralize the #1 objection (price premium) with verifiable transparency, 1,162 reviews at 97% positive, and the no-risk refund.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "2 Dogs Treats".

Brand colors: primary #1C4E7F, accent #D07832, background #FAFAF8, text #2C2C2C.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Newsletter Subscriber to First Purchase — Convert engaged newsletter subscribers who haven't yet bought into a first order, using the satisfaction guarantee as the brand's trial substitute.
- Subject: Why $20 for chicken? Open the bag and you'll get it
- Preview/preheader: 1,162 reviews, 97% positive, and a refund if your dog says no. Here's the honest math.
- Purpose: Handle the price objection head-on with proof and the guarantee — the single most decisive email for turning a curious subscriber into a buyer.
- Primary CTA: Try a bag risk-free
- Key points: Name the objection plainly: store-brand is cheaper, here's exactly what your dog isn't eating in ours | Human-grade, USA-sourced, single ingredient you can verify by reading the label — no imported mystery meat | Social proof: 1,162 reviews / 97% positive, 'vet noticed her coat,' 'same enthusiasm 9 years later' | De-risk: satisfaction guarantee = full refund if your dog doesn't love it | Nudge to free shipping over $66 with a Build-a-Box to sample multiple proteins
```

### Campaign 3: Subscription Conversion & Expansion
**Objective:** Lift LTV by converting happy one-time buyers into subscribers and expanding them into new proteins and Summit chews.  
**Rationale:** One-time buyers lapse silently and dogs reorder every 4-8 weeks — converting the post-aha buyer to subscribe-and-save is the highest-leverage retention win, and a fast one given subscription tooling already exists.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "2 Dogs Treats".

Brand colors: primary #1C4E7F, accent #D07832, background #FAFAF8, text #2C2C2C.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Subscription Conversion & Expansion — Lift LTV by converting happy one-time buyers into subscribers and expanding them into new proteins and Summit chews.
- Subject: Did Riley- I mean YOUR pup- already inhale the bag?
- Preview/preheader: Never run out, save on every order, and let your dog try a new protein on us.
- Purpose: Catch the buyer right after their dog's first rave reaction and make reordering automatic — frame subscription as never running out plus a try-a-new-protein expansion.
- Primary CTA: Set up subscribe & save
- Key points: Lead with the moment: if the first bag was a hit, you've already passed the hardest test | Subscription = never run out between the 4-8 week reorder cycle, with savings on every shipment | No contract, change or cancel anytime — same satisfaction guarantee applies | Expansion nudge: rotate proteins to beat flavor fatigue (loved Just Beef? add Just Turkey) or add a Summit chew | Multi-dog/bulk angle for high-volume households
```

### Campaign 4: Win-Back / Re-Engagement
**Objective:** Reactivate lapsed one-time buyers and dormant subscribers before they default back to supermarket treats.  
**Rationale:** Lapsed buyers are a known, warm revenue gap and win-back recovers 5-15% of inactives; a 'your pup misses these' nudge that reminds them of the clean-ingredient peace of mind is quick to ship and protects deliverability.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "2 Dogs Treats".

Brand colors: primary #1C4E7F, accent #D07832, background #FAFAF8, text #2C2C2C.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Win-Back / Re-Engagement — Reactivate lapsed one-time buyers and dormant subscribers before they default back to supermarket treats.
- Subject: Is your pup giving you the side-eye yet?
- Preview/preheader: It's been a while. Your dog's favorite single-ingredient treat is one click away.
- Purpose: Reopen the relationship by reminding the lapsed buyer of the core value their dog loved, with a frictionless one-click reorder of their go-to protein.
- Primary CTA: Reorder my pup's favorite
- Key points: Warm, no-guilt 'we miss your pup' open in the brand's neighborly voice | Remind of the value: still one ingredient, still human-grade, still made small-batch in Boston | Personalize to the protein they bought most last time for a one-click reorder | Reassurance the satisfaction guarantee still stands if they want to try something new | Soft check-in: hit reply if your dog's needs changed (new allergy, senior, picky) and we'll recommend
```

### Campaign 5: Value Newsletter
**Objective:** Stay top-of-mind and build authority on clean dog nutrition without discounting, keeping the list engaged between orders.  
**Rationale:** Blog content exists but there's no evidence of a regular value email; an always-on newsletter is the retention engine that keeps the brand present across the 4-8 week reorder gap and reinforces the ingredient-transparency authority that justifies the premium.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "2 Dogs Treats".

Brand colors: primary #1C4E7F, accent #D07832, background #FAFAF8, text #2C2C2C.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Value Newsletter — Stay top-of-mind and build authority on clean dog nutrition without discounting, keeping the list engaged between orders.
- Subject: The 3 words hiding on most 'healthy' treat labels
- Preview/preheader: If you can't pronounce it, your dog probably shouldn't eat it. Here's how to read a label.
- Purpose: Establish the repeatable hero edition: one genuinely useful ingredient-education idea, lightly tied to a product, that builds the habit of opening 2 Dogs emails.
- Primary CTA: Read the 2-minute label guide
- Key points: One useful idea per send: how to actually read a dog-treat ingredient label and spot fillers/preservatives | 80% value / 20% soft offer — teach first, then point to our single-ingredient range as the easy alternative | Recurring habit section: 'This issue's pup-nutrition tip' | Compliant framing — 'supports a healthy coat,' never disease-cure claims | Single primary CTA to the guide; reply invited with your dog's label questions
```

## Actalent Services
**URL:** https://www.actalentservices.com  
**Vertical:** B2B/professional — engineering & sciences staffing and technical services  
**Summary:** Actalent Services provides engineering and sciences staffing (contract, contract-to-hire, and direct placement) plus project-based technical services such as engineering services, clinical development, and quality/project management consulting. It serves engineering and R&D leaders, project management offices, and talent acquisition teams at mid-to-large enterprises in regulated industries — life sciences, aerospace, utilities, transportation, and semiconductor — who need specialized technical talent faster than internal recruiting can deliver. Deals are enterprise B2B, sold through account managers, with no self-serve path.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding (Employer Inquiry)
**Objective:** Activate a new employer inquiry by setting expectations, introducing the dedicated account manager, and driving toward a booked consultation call — the first-value moment.  
**Rationale:** Actalent's post-inquiry follow-up is handled manually by account managers, leaving a window where high-intent buyers cool off. An instant, human-voiced welcome that names a real account manager captures urgency and routes the buyer straight to a consultation.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Actalent Services".

Brand colors: primary #0C2D5E, accent #6B2D8B, background #FFFFFF, text #1A1A2E.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Welcome & Onboarding (Employer Inquiry) — Activate a new employer inquiry by setting expectations, introducing the dedicated account manager, and driving toward a booked consultation call — the first-value moment.
- Subject: Your engineering talent request is in — here's your next step
- Preview/preheader: A dedicated Actalent partner is already reviewing your need.
- Purpose: Confirm the inquiry was received, set expectations on what happens next, introduce the dedicated account manager by name, and deliver the first win — a booked consultation slot.
- Primary CTA: Book your consultation call
- Key points: Confirm receipt and reassure on speed — qualified candidate submittals typically begin within 48–72 hours of a defined requisition | Introduce a named account manager as a single point of contact, with a real reply-to address | Reference their stated need and timeline urgency to make it feel personally routed | One clear CTA to book the consultation; reply-to-this-email option for immediate needs
```

### Campaign 2: Consultation-to-Contract Conversion
**Objective:** Convert employer prospects who completed a free consultation but haven't yet signed an SOW or MSA by handling the cost objection and reinforcing talent-pool quality.  
**Rationale:** This is Actalent's core revenue play — the deal is closed by a human, but a structured nurture keeps the proposal alive between touchpoints. The #1 objection is staffing markup vs. direct/offshore hire, so the hero send must reframe cost as risk-and-schedule protection with proof.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Actalent Services".

Brand colors: primary #0C2D5E, accent #6B2D8B, background #FFFFFF, text #1A1A2E.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Consultation-to-Contract Conversion — Convert employer prospects who completed a free consultation but haven't yet signed an SOW or MSA by handling the cost objection and reinforcing talent-pool quality.
- Subject: What a 90-day skills gap really costs your project
- Preview/preheader: Why the right specialist beats the cheaper headcount.
- Purpose: Recap the consultation, directly address the markup-vs-direct-hire cost objection by quantifying the cost of schedule slip and mis-hires, and back it with a relevant industry case study.
- Primary CTA: Review your custom proposal
- Key points: Reframe markup as protection against schedule risk, compliance exposure, and the cost of a mis-hire in a niche discipline | Lead with a peer case study from their industry showing on-time delivery and protected margin | Reinforce talent-pool depth and vetting quality for their specific role type | Single CTA to review the proposal/SOW; offer a call with the account manager to walk through it
```

### Campaign 3: Win-Back — Dormant Clients & Candidates
**Objective:** Reactivate client accounts with no requisition in 90+ days and re-warm dormant candidate profiles before they join a competitor's roster.  
**Rationale:** Lapsed clients and a cold candidate pool are Actalent's biggest churn risks, and reactivation is fast to ship and protects deliverability. A market-intelligence hook re-opens the conversation without discounting — leading with value, which fits the B2B trust model.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Actalent Services".

Brand colors: primary #0C2D5E, accent #6B2D8B, background #FFFFFF, text #1A1A2E.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Win-Back — Dormant Clients & Candidates — Reactivate client accounts with no requisition in 90+ days and re-warm dormant candidate profiles before they join a competitor's roster.
- Subject: The engineering talent market shifted — here's what changed in your field
- Preview/preheader: A quick read for the next time a project resource gap hits.
- Purpose: Re-open the relationship with dormant client accounts using a fresh labor-market hook tied to their discipline, and offer a frictionless way to restart a requisition.
- Primary CTA: See this quarter's labor market report
- Key points: Lead with value — current hiring-difficulty and time-to-fill data for their specialty, not a sales ask | Acknowledge it's been a while and reintroduce their account manager / note any new point of contact | Remind them of the core value: specialized talent ready in days when the next project gap hits | Low-friction CTA — read the report, with a one-line option to reply and reopen a requisition
```

### Campaign 4: Lead-Magnet Nurture (Market Reports & Whitepapers)
**Objective:** Move cold leads who downloaded a market report or whitepaper toward sales-readiness across a long cycle, then route high-intent leads to the consultation play.  
**Rationale:** Actalent already produces strong lead magnets but has no evidence of a nurture series following download, so high-intent content downloaders go untouched. A buyer-journey-mapped sequence with lead scoring focuses account managers on the leads most likely to convert.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Actalent Services".

Brand colors: primary #0C2D5E, accent #6B2D8B, background #FFFFFF, text #1A1A2E.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Lead-Magnet Nurture (Market Reports & Whitepapers) — Move cold leads who downloaded a market report or whitepaper toward sales-readiness across a long cycle, then route high-intent leads to the consultation play.
- Subject: Your labor market report is inside — plus the gap most teams miss
- Preview/preheader: The data behind your hardest-to-fill engineering roles.
- Purpose: Deliver the requested asset instantly and frame the real business problem behind it — the project and compliance risk of unfilled specialized roles.
- Primary CTA: Download your report
- Key points: Deliver the downloaded asset immediately with a clean link, no friction | Frame the underlying problem the data exposes — rising time-to-fill and compliance risk in regulated disciplines | Set expectations for a short series of useful, no-fluff follow-ups over the coming weeks | Soft secondary path to a consultation for readers with an immediate need
```

### Campaign 5: Renewal & Account Expansion
**Objective:** Protect relationship-recurring revenue ahead of placement end dates and MSA reviews, and grow accounts into adjacent service lines and added headcount.  
**Rationale:** Actalent's revenue is structurally recurring through rolling contracts and renewing MSAs, and contract end-dates are a high-value, automatable gap. A value-recap send ahead of renewal quantifies the outcome delivered and opens the door to extension and adjacent service lines before a competitor does.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Actalent Services".

Brand colors: primary #0C2D5E, accent #6B2D8B, background #FFFFFF, text #1A1A2E.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Renewal & Account Expansion — Protect relationship-recurring revenue ahead of placement end dates and MSA reviews, and grow accounts into adjacent service lines and added headcount.
- Subject: Your year with Actalent, by the numbers
- Preview/preheader: Placements delivered, gaps closed, and what's next for your team.
- Purpose: Quantify the value delivered this period — placements made, roles filled, schedule risk avoided — and tee up extension plus adjacent service-line expansion.
- Primary CTA: Plan next year's talent needs
- Key points: Lead with the account's real outcomes — contractors placed, niche roles filled, time-to-fill achieved | Connect those wins to upcoming project needs and a smooth contract extension path | Surface one adjacent service line (e.g., engineering services or sciences staffing) as a natural expansion | CTA to schedule a planning review with the account manager ahead of the renewal date
```

## Affiliate Mentor
**URL:** https://www.affiliatementor.com  
**Vertical:** Education / Membership — affiliate marketing training + done-for-you list-building platform  
**Summary:** Affiliate Mentor is a tiered membership platform that pairs a done-for-you email list-building system with affiliate marketing training and a built-in commission plan. It sells a $25 Spark entry product, a $49.50/month or $397/year CORE membership (pre-built landing pages, GetResponse integration, ClickCash email monetization, workshops), and a $297/year VIP add-on. It serves aspiring online entrepreneurs and beginner-to-intermediate affiliate marketers who want a structured system to build a monetizable list and earn recurring commissions without building funnels or writing emails from scratch.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Drive activation — get a new member to their first opt-in lead or first ClickCash payout before they stall on setup.  
**Rationale:** The single biggest gap: members must connect GetResponse, configure a landing page, and activate ClickCash before the system 'works'. Without hand-holding most stall here and never reach first value — the root cause of early churn.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Affiliate Mentor".

Brand colors: primary #1A3A6B, accent #F5821F, background #FFFFFF, text #1F1F1F.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Welcome & Onboarding — Drive activation — get a new member to their first opt-in lead or first ClickCash payout before they stall on setup.
- Subject: You're in — let's get your first lead this week
- Preview/preheader: 3 steps to a live landing page (we built it for you). Start here.
- Purpose: Warm welcome, set expectations, and drive the single first setup action that leads to a first captured lead.
- Primary CTA: Connect GetResponse & activate your landing page
- Key points: Welcome by name; reassure that the system is done-for-you — they don't write emails or build funnels | One clear first action: connect GetResponse and switch on the pre-built lead-capture page so opt-ins can start flowing | Set the activation goal explicitly: your first opt-in lead (and first $0.10 ClickCash payout) is the moment it clicks | Real human reply-to offered for anyone who gets stuck on setup | FTC disclosure: results are not typical; income depends on individual effort and is not guaranteed
```

### Campaign 2: Spark-to-CORE Conversion
**Objective:** Convert $25 Spark buyers (and free resellers who upgraded) into recurring CORE members.  
**Rationale:** Spark is the paid trial; CORE is the recurring revenue engine. Buyers need a structured upgrade path that proves earnings potential AND defuses the #1 hesitation — 'is this legit or just another MLM?'  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Affiliate Mentor".

Brand colors: primary #1A3A6B, accent #F5821F, background #FFFFFF, text #1F1F1F.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Spark-to-CORE Conversion — Convert $25 Spark buyers (and free resellers who upgraded) into recurring CORE members.
- Subject: Spark got you started — here's what CORE actually unlocks
- Preview/preheader: Done-for-you pages, ClickCash, monthly workshops — and why it's not what you think.
- Purpose: Show exactly what CORE unlocks beyond Spark, back it with member proof, and answer the legitimacy objection head-on.
- Primary CTA: Upgrade to CORE membership
- Key points: Contrast Spark's one-time $50 cycle with CORE's recurring engine: pre-built pages, GetResponse automation, $0.10/click ClickCash, monthly Platinum Workshops, training vault | Address the MLM/legitimacy objection directly — real product, real list you own, transparent pricing, no hidden costs | Concrete income framing with member milestones to build aspiration without overpromising | Offer both $49.50/month and $397/year, noting the annual saves ~$200 | FTC disclosure: results are not typical; earnings depend on individual effort and are not guaranteed
```

### Campaign 3: CORE Renewal & Expansion
**Objective:** Protect recurring CORE revenue by reinforcing value before the billing date and steering monthly members to annual or VIP.  
**Rationale:** Monthly CORE churn is the biggest revenue leak — members who don't see income fast enough quietly cancel. A pre-billing value recap plus an annual-upgrade nudge is the highest-leverage retention play.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Affiliate Mentor".

Brand colors: primary #1A3A6B, accent #F5821F, background #FFFFFF, text #1F1F1F.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: CORE Renewal & Expansion — Protect recurring CORE revenue by reinforcing value before the billing date and steering monthly members to annual or VIP.
- Subject: Your month with Affiliate Mentor — and a way to save $200
- Preview/preheader: Leads captured, ClickCash earned, workshops you can still catch.
- Purpose: Quantify the value the member got this month, remove friction before billing, and present the annual upgrade as the smarter path.
- Primary CTA: Switch to annual & lock in your spot
- Key points: Recap their actual month: leads captured, ClickCash payouts, workshops attended/available, training unlocked | Remind them renewal keeps their list, landing pages, and commission eligibility live — losing access resets momentum | Position annual ($397) as saving ~$200 vs monthly and removing the monthly decision | For active earners, tease VIP ($297/yr): doubled ClickCash to $0.20/click and up to $2,500 in complimentary traffic | FTC disclosure: results are not typical; income depends on individual effort and is not guaranteed
```

### Campaign 4: Free Reseller-to-CORE Nurture
**Objective:** Move free resellers (joined the comp plan without buying) toward a paid CORE membership over a longer cycle.  
**Rationale:** Free resellers can join the compensation plan without buying anything — a large, untapped pool sitting at a capped earning ceiling. The nurture's job is to show the gap between free participation and what a real done-for-you CORE list earns.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Affiliate Mentor".

Brand colors: primary #1A3A6B, accent #F5821F, background #FFFFFF, text #1F1F1F.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Free Reseller-to-CORE Nurture — Move free resellers (joined the comp plan without buying) toward a paid CORE membership over a longer cycle.
- Subject: Why free resellers hit a wall (and how members get past it)
- Preview/preheader: Same effort, very different ceiling. Here's the difference CORE makes.
- Purpose: Evaluation-stage proof email — show how a member like them broke past the free-reseller ceiling with the CORE system.
- Primary CTA: See what CORE unlocks
- Key points: Name the ceiling: free participation has limited earning ability — effort without the done-for-you list-building engine behind it | Show a relatable member story moving from cold traffic to a list they own with consistent opt-ins | Tie the upgrade to their pain: inconsistent traffic, low commissions, technical overwhelm — all handled by CORE's pre-built system | Low-friction next step framed as exploring, not a hard pitch, given the long consideration cycle | FTC disclosure: results are not typical; earnings depend on individual effort and are not guaranteed
```

### Campaign 5: Lapsed Member Win-Back
**Objective:** Reactivate cancelled or dormant members — especially those who stalled before their first win — and clean the list.  
**Rationale:** The core churn story is 'joined for income, stalled on setup, saw no results in 60–90 days, cancelled.' These contacts already wanted the outcome — a 'we'll get you to first value this time' reactivation recovers 5–15% and protects deliverability.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Affiliate Mentor".

Brand colors: primary #1A3A6B, accent #F5821F, background #FFFFFF, text #1F1F1F.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Lapsed Member Win-Back — Reactivate cancelled or dormant members — especially those who stalled before their first win — and clean the list.
- Subject: Still want a list that earns while you sleep?
- Preview/preheader: Most who left stalled on setup. Let's fix that in one sitting.
- Purpose: Reopen the relationship by acknowledging the stall and offering a fast, guided path to the first win they never reached.
- Primary CTA: Reactivate & finish your setup
- Key points: Empathetic open: many members stall before the system clicks — no judgment, the door's still open | Remind them of the core value they signed up for: a monetizable list they own and ClickCash payouts | Lead with help, not guilt — offer a guided setup so they reach their first opt-in lead this time | Note what's new/improved since they left to give a concrete reason to return | FTC disclosure: results are not typical; income depends on individual effort and is not guaranteed
```

## AI for Christians
**URL:** https://aiforchristians.ai  
**Vertical:** Education/nonprofit/membership (faith-based digital education)  
**Summary:** AI for Christians publishes low-ticket ($3–$7) books and bookazines plus free Bible-study and spiritual-warfare AI chatbots, a free 'Digital Discipleship' newsletter, and a free community — all teaching Christians to use AI for ministry, discipleship, and daily life without compromising their faith. It serves evangelical and Pentecostal believers (pastors, ministry leaders, students, and devout laypeople) who feel both drawn to and fearful of AI. The whole catalog exists to dismantle one objection: that AI is spiritually dangerous or at odds with following God.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Get every new newsletter, community, or chatbot sign-up to the 'aha' moment — experiencing faith and AI working together — within their first session.  
**Rationale:** These are free-signup contacts caught between two fears, and the activation path (free chatbot or a $3 book) is immediate and self-serve — a fast instant welcome turns curiosity into a first faith+AI win before doubt creeps back in.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "AI for Christians".

Brand colors: primary #7B2D8B, accent #C9A227, background #0F0F1A, text #F5F0E8.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Welcome & Onboarding — Get every new newsletter, community, or chatbot sign-up to the 'aha' moment — experiencing faith and AI working together — within their first session.
- Subject: You're in — now let's prove AI can serve your walk with God
- Preview/preheader: Two minutes with one free tool, and the fear starts to lift.
- Purpose: Warm welcome, set the Spirit-Led + AI-Assisted promise, and deliver one immediate proof-of-concept win via a free tool.
- Primary CTA: Open the Logos Bible Study AI (free)
- Key points: Welcome them and name the tension head-on: you can lead in the AI age without compromising your faith | Hand them one quick win now — a free Poe chatbot (Logos Bible Study AI) so they feel faith and AI working together in minutes | Set expectations for the short series ahead and invite a real reply — a real person reads every one
```

### Campaign 2: Lead-Magnet Nurture
**Objective:** Move free subscribers who haven't bought past the 'AI is spiritually dangerous' objection and toward their first $3–$7 book or bookazine.  
**Rationale:** This brand's entire reason to exist is dismantling one objection, so the highest-leverage nurture send is the one that reconciles AI with Scripture — clearing the only real barrier between a free subscriber and a $3–$7 purchase.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "AI for Christians".

Brand colors: primary #7B2D8B, accent #C9A227, background #0F0F1A, text #F5F0E8.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Lead-Magnet Nurture — Move free subscribers who haven't bought past the 'AI is spiritually dangerous' objection and toward their first $3–$7 book or bookazine.
- Subject: Is AI spiritually dangerous? Let's settle it with Scripture
- Preview/preheader: The honest answer most won't give you about AI and your faith.
- Purpose: Confront the #1 objection directly with a biblical, doctrinally-sensitive framework, then bridge to the entry-priced book that goes deeper.
- Primary CTA: Read "AI JUST Killed the Theologian" ($5)
- Key points: Name the fear without flinching: AI as idol vs. AI as tool — the difference is who you serve with it | Give a Scripture-grounded framework for stewarding AI in ministry, staying neutral on divisive doctrinal lines | Bridge to the $5 book as the next, low-risk step for readers who want the full case
```

### Campaign 3: Win-Back / Re-Engagement
**Objective:** Reactivate dormant subscribers and one-off buyers with a low-barrier re-entry, and clean the list to protect deliverability.  
**Rationale:** With one-off purchases and a free community, there's no automatic pull-back mechanism, so dormant contacts quietly leak away — a Kingdom-urgency win-back is quick to ship and recovers 5–15% before they're lost.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "AI for Christians".

Brand colors: primary #7B2D8B, accent #C9A227, background #0F0F1A, text #F5F0E8.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Win-Back / Re-Engagement — Reactivate dormant subscribers and one-off buyers with a low-barrier re-entry, and clean the list to protect deliverability.
- Subject: Did we lose you — or did the noise just get loud?
- Preview/preheader: The AI moment isn't slowing down. Your church still needs you leading it.
- Purpose: Re-open the relationship by reminding them of the stakes (leading, not falling behind) and offering a frictionless free return path.

## BOP TV (Black on Purpose Television Network)
**URL:** https://www.boptv.com  
**Vertical:** Streaming media / Entertainment / Membership  
**Summary:** BOP TV is a Black-owned subscription streaming network offering 30+ channels of Black-created films, TV shows, cartoons, documentaries, and originals for $12.99/month or $99.99/year. It serves Black Americans and the global African diaspora (roughly 25-55) who feel underserved by mainstream platforms and want positive, culturally resonant content free of negative stereotypes. Secondary revenue comes from advertising packages for Black businesses, distribution for independent creators, production services, and a media-arts training center.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Get a new subscriber streaming their first culturally resonant show within 48-72 hours, before passive churn sets in.  
**Rationale:** With 30+ channels and no guided tour, new subscribers stall at the catalog and lapse before the aha moment of finding content they can't get anywhere else. Onboarding is BOP TV's single most critical and highest-leverage gap.

## Boyum Law
**URL:** https://www.boyumlaw.com  
**Vertical:** Local & service / B2B professional (legal — estate planning & probate)  
**Summary:** Boyum Law is a solo, Nebraska-licensed law firm in the Omaha metro (attorney Brad Boyum) handling estate planning — wills, living trusts, special needs and pet trusts, farm succession, and asset protection — plus probate administration, elder law, powers of attorney, and Medicaid planning. It serves Omaha-area families aged roughly 45–70 with accumulated assets who haven't formalized a plan, and adult children or spouses navigating probate after a death. Engagements are one-off, project-based legal fees, and the free initial consultation is the primary way clients are won.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Turn a new inquiry or consultation request into a confident, prepared lead who shows up to the free consultation knowing exactly what to expect.  
**Rationale:** Every backbone campaign is missing today, so the playbook's #1 priority applies cleanly: this is the highest-engagement, fastest-to-value send and it sets the trust that a sensitive, family-first legal purchase depends on. For Boyum, the inquiry-to-consultation moment is where intent is hottest and where most leads currently fall silent.  

**Email Prompt:**

```

THIS EMAIL:

- Subject: We got your message — here's what your free consultation covers
- Preview/preheader: No legal jargon, no obligation. Just a clear plan for protecting your family.
- Purpose: Instant warm welcome the moment someone reaches out: reassure them, set expectations for the free consultation, and deliver one quick win (clarity on what the meeting covers and that there is zero obligation).
- Primary CTA: Confirm your free consultation time
- Key points: Reassure: reaching out is the hard part, and there's no cost and no obligation to retain after the consultation | Set expectations for the 30–60 min meeting with Brad — he reviews your specific situation and shows you exactly which documents (will, trust, POA) you actually need and why | Tell them what to bring (rough list of assets, who they'd name) so the meeting is productive | Plain-English, family-first tone; a real reply-to (Brad/firm) and the firm name + Omaha address for CAN-SPAM and NE Bar compliance | Disclaimer: this email does not create an attorney-client relationship
```

### Campaign 2: Free-Consultation Conversion

**Rationale:** The free consultation is Boyum's entire close mechanism, so the core revenue play (playbook #2) is to get unbooked leads into that meeting. The single biggest blocker is 'do I really need a lawyer, or is LegalZoom enough?' — answering that with candor is what moves an Omaha family from curious to committed.  

**Email Prompt:**

```

## Brooklyn Spectacles
**URL:** https://www.brooklynspectacles.com  
**Vertical:** Local & service — independent eyewear retail (DTC + brick-and-mortar)  
**Summary:** Brooklyn Spectacles is an independent eyewear brand that designs and hand-finishes optical frames, sunglasses, and a children's line ('Little Spectacles') in Italian acetate at its Williamsburg, Brooklyn studio. It sells direct-to-consumer online and at its flagship at 291 Bedford Ave, plus through authorized US and Canada retailers, serving style-conscious urban creatives and professionals who want distinctive, well-made frames over mass-market chain eyewear. Purchases are one-off (roughly $195–$225 per frame) with a natural 1–3 year repeat cycle driven by prescription changes, frame wear, or wanting a new look.

## Clarusway
**URL:** https://www.clarusway.com  
**Vertical:** Education / IT Bootcamp  
**Summary:** Clarusway is an online IT bootcamp that retrains career changers with no tech background into job-ready professionals in Cloud & DevOps, Data Science & AI, Full Stack Development, Salesforce, Cybersecurity, and more over 3-8 months of part-time study. Programs cost $7,000-$8,000 with flexible financing (ISA, installments, 30% upfront discount) and the company markets an outcome: graduates reportedly land tech jobs averaging $90K-$102K. Its funnel runs on free lead magnets (a 50+ hour mini bootcamp, a career-path quiz, info sessions) feeding advisor-assisted consultations that close enrollments.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Get a new free signup to their first hands-on win — running their first line of code — proving to a total beginner that tech is learnable for someone like them.

### Campaign 3: Booking Reminders & No-Show Recovery

## Frog Music Press
**URL:** https://www.frogmusic.com  
**Vertical:** Education/nonprofit/membership  
**Summary:** Frog Music Press, led by organist Noel Jones (AAGO) out of Augusta, KY, publishes Catholic liturgical music resources: organ and choir books, Gregorian chant guides, MIDI organ files, the PTCO series for Rodgers and Roland digital organs, and a 14-week Free Chant School. Materials are distributed mostly as free PDF downloads (with a donation ask) plus low-cost Amazon paperbacks and Kindle editions. It serves amateur and part-time Catholic parish organists and choir directors who need affordable, liturgically accurate music without formal training.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Get a new free-download subscriber to their first 'aha' — successfully singing or playing one chant or hymn — within the first week, then frame future donations and books around the mission.  
**Rationale:** The brand's biggest leak is that free users grab one PDF and vanish with no follow-up; an instant welcome that delivers a quick win is the single highest-leverage flow to convert anonymous downloaders into engaged, eventually-donating parish musicians.

- Key points: State the deadline and the stakes plainly in-persona: early access ends, edition is limited/numbered, this is the subscribers-first reward for being on the signal | Reinforce the value and remove friction: what the drop is, why it matters to a retro-tech collector, one button to the checkout/claim page, offer help via reply | Add a human/urgency close ('I do not reopen sealed drops') and a fallback nudge for the cold branch referencing they viewed but didn't claim
```

### Campaign 5: Win-Back — Signal Lost
**Objective:** undefined  
**Rationale:** Quick to ship and it protects sender reputation as the list grows — for a brand with no purchase data, a dormant subscriber is pure deliverability risk, and the persona's 'fading signal' framing makes the re-engagement ask feel native rather than desperate.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "IAmComput0r".

Brand colors: primary #d4c9a8, accent #00ff44, background #1a1a1a, text #5a4f35.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Win-Back — Signal Lost — undefined
- Subject: Y0UR SIGNAL IS FADING. C0ME BACK BEF0RE I G0 DARK.
- Preview/preheader: I haven't heard from you in a while. One click keeps the connection alive.
- Purpose: Reopen the relationship with a pattern-interrupt 'we miss you' in-persona — remind them of the core value (the aesthetic, the lore, the artifacts) and give one low-friction reason to re-engage before the sunset steps begin.
- Primary CTA: RECONNECT TO THE MACHINE
- Key points: In-persona 'we miss you': the machine has been transmitting into static — remind them what the signal carries (retro lore, artifact drops, the world they joined) | One frictionless re-engagement action: re-experience the boot sequence or grab the latest artifact — a single click that re-flags them as active | Set up the sunset: signal that if the connection stays silent the machine will eventually stop transmitting (protects deliverability), making this a genuine last-value moment
```

## IAmH3r

Acquisition is social-first (X/Twitter, likely Instagram); the likely revenue model is a free community feeding paid membership, coaching, or digital products. Note: the brand site was not resolving at research time, so offer structure, pricing, and tooling remain unconfirmed and should be validated at client kickoff.

**Objective:** Deliver the 'I Am Her' moment immediately — make a new subscriber feel seen, introduce the founder and community, and drive the first affirmation/community action.  
**Rationale:** Every gap is unconfirmed, but for a social-first personal brand the welcome is the highest-engagement, fastest-to-show-value send and the moment to convert a curious follower into a member of the sisterhood before the spark fades.

## Jeenie Jolie
**URL:** https://jeeniejolie.com  
**Vertical:** DTC organic / artisanal skincare & body care (wellness & beauty)  
**Summary:** Jeenie Jolie is a direct-to-consumer brand selling organic, artisanal skincare and body care — tallow-based face cream, whipped body butters, body oils, African black soap, shea butter, sugar scrubs, and natural loofahs, plus bundles. It serves women aged 25–45 who want clean, natural products and frame self-care as intentional, spiritual ritual rather than routine. All revenue comes from one-time purchases; there is no subscription or membership tier.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Bridge the gap between purchase and first use so the customer reaches the 'aha' moment — the texture, scent, and skin-feel of their first product — and trusts the brand enough to reorder.  
**Rationale:** There is no guided onboarding today — likely just a Shopify order confirmation — so new buyers are left to figure out the product alone, and a clean tallow/natural formula needs expectation-setting to overcome the brand's #1 objection. A warm, ritual-led welcome converts skepticism into a confident first use and seeds the repeat purchase.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Jeenie Jolie".

Brand colors: primary #1C1A17, accent #C9A84C, background #0F0E0C, text #F5F0E8.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Welcome & Onboarding — Bridge the gap between purchase and first use so the customer reaches the 'aha' moment — the texture, scent, and skin-feel of their first product — and trusts the brand enough to reorder.
- Subject: Welcome to the ritual, beautiful — your glow is on its way
- Preview/preheader: A few words to prepare your skin (and your senses) before it arrives.
- Purpose: Warm welcome the moment the order is placed: set expectations for the natural texture and scent, frame the product as a ritual, and give one simple first action so the first use lands as an 'aha' rather than a surprise.
- Primary CTA: Read your ritual guide
- Key points: Set honest expectations: tallow cream and whipped butters feel and smell different from synthetic drugstore products — that's the clean formula at work | Frame first use as a ritual: warm a small amount between palms, breathe, apply with intention rather than rushing | One simple first action — open the ritual guide and choose a moment (morning light or evening wind-down) for the first application | Reassure with the brand promise (organic, intentional, made in small batches) and invite a real reply if they have questions — using 'nourishes/soothes' language, never drug claims
```

### Campaign 2: 30% Welcome Offer Nurture
**Objective:** Convert an email signup into a first purchase by delivering the 30% code (HAPPY30) and nurturing undecided subscribers past the natural-vs-mainstream skepticism objection.  
**Rationale:** With no free trial, the 30% code is the brand's core conversion mechanism, yet it is likely sent once with no follow-up if unredeemed. A short nurture that re-presents the offer with ingredient education and ritual framing is the single highest-leverage way to lift first-purchase rate from existing signups.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Jeenie Jolie".

- Preview/preheader: Code HAPPY30 inside. Your glow starts with one mindful choice.
- Purpose: Deliver the 30% code instantly, frame the discount as an invitation into a clean-beauty ritual rather than a transaction, and point to the bestselling hero product to remove choice paralysis.
- Primary CTA: Shop with HAPPY30
- Key points: Deliver code HAPPY30 prominently with the 30%-off-first-order terms clear | Lead with the hero tallow face cream and a best-for-beginners body butter so the first choice is easy | Address the top objection up front: why organic tallow and whipped shea nourish skin better than silicone-heavy mainstream formulas (no drug claims) | Reinforce the ritual identity — clean ingredients, small-batch, intentional self-care — and signal gentle urgency that the welcome offer is for the first order
```

### Campaign 3: Replenishment & Cross-Sell
**Objective:** Drive the second order by reminding buyers to replenish before they run out and introducing a complementary SKU or bundle to grow order value.  
**Rationale:** Revenue depends entirely on repeat purchase but no replenishment or cross-sell flow exists, leaving the brand reliant on customers remembering to reorder. A timed 'running low' + pairing nudge is the biggest second revenue lever for a product brand with no subscription.

```

- Primary CTA: Reorder + complete your ritual
- Key points: Assume the product is near-empty at the replenishment window and make the exact reorder one tap | Cross-sell the natural pairing for what they bought (e.g., face cream → body oil; body butter → sugar scrub for prep) | Frame the second product as deepening the ritual, not upselling — layering for head-to-toe nourishment | Offer a small bundle-the-two incentive or free-shipping threshold to nudge the larger order
```

## Karen's Botanicals
**URL:** https://www.karensbotanicals.com  
**Vertical:** Organic skincare & wellness (ecommerce)  
**Summary:** Karen's Botanicals handcrafts organic skincare and bodycare products — cleansers, toners, creams, serums, oils, balms, and herbal health tonics — in small batches on the Mitchell family farm in Georgia, using 19th-century Slovak botanical recipes. It serves health-conscious women roughly 35–65 who distrust mass-market, chemical-laden beauty products and want clean, ingredient-transparent alternatives that respect aging naturally. Sales are one-off self-serve purchases (no subscription) on its own site and Amazon, with repeat buying driven by a points-based rewards program.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Convert a new email subscriber into a confident first purchase and get them to the 'aha' moment — the first use where clean, farm-made skincare visibly outperforms what they used before.  
**Rationale:** Every backbone flow is currently missing and the model is fully self-serve, so a new subscriber who doesn't learn the heritage story, correct routine, and skin-type match will never reach the aha moment and won't return. The welcome send is the highest-engagement, fastest-win lever the brand has.  

**Email Prompt:**

```

- Preview/preheader: Two generations, one Georgia farm, and the first step for your skin.
- Purpose: Warm welcome + deliver the 10% code + tell the farm/heritage story + point to the one first action (match a skin type via the Facial Care Chart).
- Primary CTA: Find your skin-type match & shop 10% off
- Key points: Deliver the 10%-off welcome code prominently with a clear expiry | Tell the origin story in the brand's voice: 19th-century Slovak recipes, handcrafted in small batches on the Mitchell family farm in Georgia | Single first action — use the Facial Care Chart to match their skin type to the right cleanser/serum/moisturizer | Set expectations: a few short emails over the next two weeks on routine and results, and that a real person reads every reply | Reassure on purity — what's never in the products (synthetic fillers, parabens) to pre-empt the price-premium doubt
```

### Campaign 2: Lead-Magnet Nurture
**Objective:** Move a subscriber who took the 10% coupon but hasn't purchased toward a first order by defusing the #1 objection — 'is the premium worth it vs. a drugstore product?'  
**Rationale:** The brand's stated top objection is price premium and small-batch skepticism, and acquisition (SEO, Amazon, rewards) brings in subscribers who stall on that exact doubt. A proof-and-transparency email reframes the cost before the coupon expires.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Karen's Botanicals".

Brand colors: primary #4A7C59, accent #C5883C, background #F5F0E8, text #2D2416.

- Purpose: Handle the price-premium objection head-on by reframing cost around ingredient transparency and what is deliberately left out, backed by substantiated proof.
- Primary CTA: See what's inside (and what isn't)
- Key points: Reframe price: a $26 serum with named botanical ingredients vs. a $10 formula padded with synthetic fillers — cost-per-honest-ingredient, not cost-per-ounce | Lead with ingredient transparency: every ingredient readable and sourced, small-batch on the farm | Use substantiated 'clinically validated' proof and real customer results — stay within FTC efficacy-claim limits (no treat/cure language) | Spotlight one accessible best-seller matched to their skin-type interest as a low-risk first buy | Remind the 10%-off code is still active with a gentle expiry nudge

**Rationale:** This is the brand's single biggest gap: consumables cycle every 4–8 weeks but there is no auto-replenishment, so customers silently drift between cycles. A timed refill-plus-routine nudge is the most revenue-proximate flow for a no-subscription repeat-purchase model.

## NBCOS — National Board for Certification in the Orthopedic Specialties
**URL:** https://www.nbcos.org  
**Vertical:** Education / Nonprofit / Membership (professional credentialing)  
**Summary:** NBCOS is a not-for-profit credentialing body that administers board-recognized specialty certification exams (OPE-C, OPE-SC, OPE-Radiography, ROT) and a 150+ course continuing-education library for orthopedic allied health professionals, bundled into a $179/year Full Membership. Its core audience is Certified Athletic Trainers who need a documented orthopedic specialty credential to compete for clinical roles across orthopedic offices, hospitals, and urgent care centers. Revenue is recurring annual membership, sustained by a two-year CEU reporting cycle and credential-stacking expansion toward the OPE-CS Clinical Specialist designation.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding — Signup to Exam Pass
**Objective:** Drive new members from signup to their first real value: passing the OPE-C exam and earning the board credential.  
**Rationale:** NBCOS's aha moment is passing the OPE-C exam and downloading the credential — but study is self-directed, so without an onboarding sequence new members stall before sitting the exam and never reach the value they paid for. This is the highest-engagement, fastest-to-show-a-win flow.

- Key points: Confirm membership is active: exam registration, the OPE Candidate Guide, and 150+ Category A CEUs are all unlocked now | One clear first action — open the Candidate Guide and run the sample exam questions to gauge readiness | Set the goal plainly: pass the OPE-C exam (125 questions, 70% to pass) and put the board credential on your résumé and LinkedIn | Real human reply-to for exam or study questions; preview the short onboarding emails to come

Crew, management, maintenance, and charter brokerage are bundled, and a separate charter business lets prospects experience the fleet before buying. ## NinjaClick
**URL:** https://www.ninjaclick.com  
**Vertical:** SaaS/tech — visitor intelligence  
**Summary:** NinjaClick is a SaaS visitor-intelligence platform: a single line of JavaScript identifies up to 80% of a website's anonymous visitors — surfacing company details and decision-maker contact info without forms or cookies. It serves B2B marketing, demand-gen, and sales teams (plus DTC brands) who want to turn anonymous, high-intent traffic into a contactable pipeline. Sold as a self-serve monthly subscription with a permanent free tier and a 14-day no-card trial, tiered by monthly identity volume.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Drive activation — get the new trial user to install the JS snippet and see their first batch of identified visitors (the aha moment) inside the 14-day window.  
**Rationale:** NinjaClick's entire value is visceral and instant — but only after the snippet is live. Users who never install never see identified visitors and churn immediately, so the highest-leverage email moves them to install on day 0.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "NinjaClick".

Brand colors: primary #111827, accent #6C47FF, background #FFFFFF, text #111827.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Welcome & Onboarding — Drive activation — get the new trial user to install the JS snippet and see their first batch of identified visitors (the aha moment) inside the 14-day window.
- Subject: Your snippet's ready — see who's on your site today
- Preview/preheader: One line of JavaScript. First identified visitors in minutes.
- Purpose: Warm welcome, set the one goal of the trial, and deliver the single fastest first win: paste the snippet so identified visitors start appearing.
- Primary CTA: Install your tracking snippet
- Key points: One job for today: paste your unique JS snippet into your site — copy/paste or send the 2-line guide to your developer | What happens next: real names, companies, and job titles of your visitors start landing in your dashboard within minutes to a few hours | Reassure on the #1 objection up front — GDPR-compliant, consent-based identification, no covert tracking | Human reply-to: stuck on install? Reply and a real person helps you get live before the trial clock runs
```

### Campaign 2: Trial-to-Paid Conversion
**Objective:** Convert activated trial users into a paid Growth/Scale plan before the 14-day window closes, and prevent loss of the leads they've already identified.  
**Rationale:** Trial-to-paid is the core revenue metric for a self-serve SaaS with a hard 14-day window. The expiry email tied to the user's own identified-visitor count is the most persuasive send NinjaClick can make.

- Purpose: Expiry warning anchored to the user's real results — quantify the visitors they identified and frame upgrading as keeping that pipeline alive.
- Primary CTA: Pick your plan & keep your data
- Key points: Lead with their own numbers: '{count} visitors identified across {company_count} companies in 14 days' — proof the match rate is real for their traffic | Make the loss concrete — when the trial ends, identification pauses and new high-intent visitors go back to anonymous | Right-size the plan: Growth $97/mo to start, Scale $497/mo at 10,000 identities; no contract, cancel anytime | Offer a human path for Enterprise volume or integration questions — book a call instead of guessing

### Campaign 3: Booking, Reminders & No-Show Recovery
**Objective:** Maximize attended meetings/appointments and recover the ones that slip.

## Paymentum Payment Solutions
**URL:** https://www.paymentum.net  
**Vertical:** B2B/professional — merchant services / fintech  
**Summary:** Paymentum is a Nashville-based merchant services and payment processing company that helps small-to-mid-sized businesses eliminate or sharply reduce the 3-4% they lose to card processing fees, primarily through compliant surcharging and dual-pricing programs plus omni-channel POS hardware, terminals, gateways, and ACH. It serves healthcare practices, restaurants, and retail merchants on month-to-month terms with no long-term contract, and earns on ongoing transaction volume. Deals close through an assisted, rep-led path: a free payments audit or savings-calculator result leads to a booked demo and a side-by-side savings proposal before a merchant agreement is signed.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Get a newly-signed merchant from agreement to their first live transaction at 0% net cost — the activation moment that confirms the promise and prevents early silent churn.  
**Rationale:** Paymentum's sale is assisted and the 'aha' is operational — seeing 0% net cost on a live transaction — so a confident, supported first-week is the single highest-leverage build, and unactivated merchants are the biggest silent-churn risk.

- Key points: Welcome the owner by name and restate the promise: keep the 3-4% you were handing to the card networks | One clear first action — activate the terminal / run a test transaction — framed as a 2-minute step with rep support on standby | Set the 'aha' expectation: see 0% net cost on your next statement, and reply to this email to reach a real person on the onboarding team

## Pinnacle Investments
**URL:** https://www.pinnacle-investments.com  
**Vertical:** B2B/professional — financial services (mortgage note buying)  
**Summary:** Pinnacle Investments buys seller-financed mortgage notes, trust deeds, land contracts, and promissory notes from private note holders nationwide, paying a lump sum in exchange for the future payment stream. It serves individuals — often retirees and accidental note holders — who owner-financed a property sale and now want immediate cash instead of waiting years on monthly payments. The entry point is a free, no-obligation note analysis that produces a customized written offer, with closing through a title company in roughly 10–15 working days.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Turn a free-quote / note-analysis request into an engaged prospect who reaches first value — a concrete written offer — by setting expectations, building trust, and removing the friction that makes prospects go cold.  
**Rationale:** This is the brand's biggest gap and where most prospects go cold — there is no formal sequence after a quote request, yet the entire transaction hinges on getting from inquiry to a written offer while trust is still warm.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Pinnacle Investments".

Brand colors: primary #0D2B55, accent #C9963C, background #FFFFFF, text #1F2937.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Welcome & Onboarding — Turn a free-quote / note-analysis request into an engaged prospect who reaches first value — a concrete written offer — by setting expectations, building trust, and removing the friction that makes prospects go cold.
- Subject: Your free note analysis is underway — here's what happens next
- Preview/preheader: An advisor reviews your note, then sends a real dollar offer — usually within a few days.
- Purpose: Instant warm welcome that confirms the request, sets a clear timeline to the written offer, and delivers the first win: reassurance that the process is safe, free, and obligation-free.
- Primary CTA: Reply with your note details (or upload them) so we can price your offer
- Key points: Confirm the request landed and a certified planner is already reviewing it; set the expectation of advisor contact within 1 business day and a written offer within a few days of receiving note documents | Build trust up front with credibility markers: 26 years in business, 22,000+ notes purchased, 8 certified planners, closing through a title company in 10–15 working days | Make the single first action obvious — send the note details we need (note type, balance, interest rate, payment history) so the offer is accurate and fast | Reassure: the analysis is free, no obligation to accept, and they keep collecting payments until they choose to sell; reply-to is a real advisor | Footer disclosure that Pinnacle is a note buyer, not a licensed broker-dealer, and that the email is not investment advice (CAN-SPAM compliant)
```

### Campaign 2: Quote-to-Offer Conversion
**Objective:** Convert prospects who requested a quote — or already received a written offer — into accepted offers by reinforcing the value of the number, handling the fair-price objection head-on, and giving a clear, low-friction path to say yes.  
**Rationale:** The stated primary goal is improving quote-to-close conversion, and the #1 objection — 'is the discount too steep / will I get a fair price?' — is exactly what kills these deals, so the core revenue play is an offer-reinforcement email that defends the number.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Pinnacle Investments".

Brand colors: primary #0D2B55, accent #C9963C, background #FFFFFF, text #1F2937.

THIS EMAIL:

- Subject: Your note offer — and exactly how we arrived at the number
- Preview/preheader: Fair value, explained line by line. No obligation, and the offer still stands.
- Purpose: Re-present the written offer and disarm the fair-value objection by transparently explaining how the number was reached, then make accepting frictionless.

## Powerful Wellness

It offers a free 15-minute discovery call, ongoing 1-on-1 coaching, a structured 6-week program across five health pillars (including medical/metabolic options like GLP-1, LIPOLEAN, and peptides), and digital products. ## Ray Media
**URL:** https://www.raymedia.cc  
**Vertical:** B2B/professional services — digital marketing agency  
**Summary:** Ray Media is a boutique digital marketing agency that sells SEO, video marketing, lead generation, and social media management as monthly retainers to small and medium businesses. It serves local service businesses and online entrepreneurs who have a product worth selling but lack the digital presence or expertise to generate consistent inbound leads. Its entire funnel converges on a single free discovery/strategy call that closes to a custom proposal and an ongoing retainer.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Activate a newly signed retainer client by setting clear expectations, establishing the approval-and-feedback loop, and framing the SEO ramp timeline so they don't churn before results compound.  
**Rationale:** Ray Media's #1 churn risk is the 'patience gap' — clients cancel in months 1–2 because SEO takes 3–6 months to pay off. The welcome email is the one place to pre-frame that timeline and lock in trust before doubt sets in.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Ray Media".

Brand colors: primary #1B2E4B, accent #F5A623, background #F8F9FA, text #212529.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Welcome & Onboarding — Activate a newly signed retainer client by setting clear expectations, establishing the approval-and-feedback loop, and framing the SEO ramp timeline so they don't churn before results compound.
- Subject: You're in — here's your roadmap to getting seen
- Preview/preheader: Your first 60 days with Ray Media, step by step — plus the one thing we need from you.
- Purpose: Warm welcome, set the 60-day expectation, show the first quick win, and establish what Ray Media needs from the client.
- Primary CTA: Review your 60-day game plan
- Key points: Reframe the timeline up front: quick-win tactics surface in 30–60 days, compounding SEO lift lands in months 3–6 — so early patience is the strategy, not a delay | Deliver an instant win: the initial visibility audit / baseline so they see value on day one | Set the feedback loop clearly — your only jobs are to approve content fast and answer the phone when leads come in | Open a real reply-to channel ('hit reply, Ray reads every one') to build founder-level trust early
```

### Campaign 2: Discovery-Call to Retainer Conversion
**Objective:** Convert a completed free discovery call into a signed retainer by delivering the custom proposal and dismantling the ROI-skepticism objection.  
**Rationale:** The whole business bottlenecks at the consult, and the proposal email is the literal revenue moment. Ray Media's top objection — 'we paid for marketing before and it didn't work' — must be answered here with proof, or the deal stalls.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Ray Media".

Brand colors: primary #1B2E4B, accent #F5A623, background #F8F9FA, text #212529.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Discovery-Call to Retainer Conversion — Convert a completed free discovery call into a signed retainer by delivering the custom proposal and dismantling the ROI-skepticism objection.
- Subject: Your custom growth plan is inside, {{firstName}}
- Preview/preheader: Exactly how we'll get you seen — and what it's worth to your bottom line.
- Purpose: Deliver the custom growth plan tied to the call, quantify the upside, and neutralize the ROI objection with a relevant result.
- Primary CTA: Approve your plan & book kickoff
- Key points: Recap their exact goal from the call so the plan feels built for them, not boilerplate | Lay out the specific services and the 30/60/90-day milestones tied to lead and ranking outcomes | Hit the ROI objection head-on with a comparable business result — 'here's what happened for a business like yours' | Lower the risk: clarify the month-to-month commitment and a single, friction-free next step to start
```

### Campaign 3: Call Reminders & No-Show Recovery
**Objective:** Maximize attended discovery calls and instantly recover the ones that slip, protecting the single highest-leverage event in the funnel.  
**Rationale:** Every no-show is a lost retainer, and reminders cut no-shows by ~35%. For a founder-led agency where the call is the only conversion event, a day-before reminder is the cheapest revenue Ray Media can capture.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Ray Media".

Brand colors: primary #1B2E4B, accent #F5A623, background #F8F9FA, text #212529.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Call Reminders & No-Show Recovery — Maximize attended discovery calls and instantly recover the ones that slip, protecting the single highest-leverage event in the funnel.
- Subject: Your strategy call is tomorrow at {{time}} — one thing to bring
- Preview/preheader: Five minutes of prep turns this into a call that actually moves your leads.
- Purpose: Day-before reminder that confirms the time, primes the prospect to show up prepared, and offers a one-tap reschedule instead of a silent no-show.
- Primary CTA: Confirm or reschedule
- Key points: Restate the date, time, and join/dial-in details so attending is effortless | Give one piece of prep — 'come with your #1 lead goal' — which both raises show-up intent and makes the call convert better | Offer a no-penalty one-click reschedule link to convert would-be no-shows into a kept slot | Reinforce the payoff of showing up: a free, tailored plan to get found on Google with no obligation
```

### Campaign 4: Get Seen Newsletter
**Objective:** Stay top-of-mind with leads and keep active clients engaged during the slow SEO ramp by delivering one useful visibility tip per send — building authority without discounting.  
**Rationale:** A regular value email does double duty for Ray Media: it nurtures the leads who haven't booked yet and keeps signed clients engaged through the months-1–2 patience gap, directly countering the early-churn risk while reinforcing expertise.  

**Email Prompt:**

```

- Primary CTA: Get your free visibility audit

**Objective:** Protect monthly recurring revenue and grow accounts by quantifying the results each client got and teeing up the single-service-to-bundle upsell.

## RCA Tax Services
**URL:** https://rcataxservices.com  
**Vertical:** B2B/professional — year-round tax planning & advisory for high-income earners and business owners  
**Summary:** RCA Tax Services is a Santa Ana, CA firm (serving clients nationwide) that provides proactive, year-round tax planning and strategy — not just filing — for high earners and business owners paying $80K+ a year in taxes. It serves physicians, attorneys, real estate investors, tech executives with equity comp, consultants, and entrepreneurs earning roughly $500K–$5M, using strategies like entity structuring, cost segregation, retirement-plan design, and capital-gains planning to legally lower their effective tax rate. The engagement starts with a free 30-minute consultation with Ray and typically converts into an ongoing advisory retainer.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding — Lead to Booked Consult
**Objective:** Turn a new lead (blog reader, referral, or ad click) into a booked free 30-minute consultation with Ray — the brand's single activation event.  
**Rationale:** RCA's entire 'aha' depends on a booked, attended consult where Ray quantifies the dollars left on the table. With no existing welcome flow, this is the highest-leverage build — it converts anonymous interest into the firm's one revenue-starting action.

- Subject: If you pay $80K+ in taxes, you're likely overpaying — let's find out by how much
- Preview/preheader: A free 30 minutes with Ray shows you the exact strategies your CPA isn't using.
- Purpose: Instant warm welcome that lands the 'you're almost certainly overpaying' hook and drives to book the free consult with one clear CTA.
- Primary CTA: Book your free 30-minute consultation with Ray
- Key points: Lead with the core promise: a CPA files your return; RCA plans around you to legally cut your effective rate 10–40%. | Make the cost of inaction tangible — high earners routinely overpay five and six figures on strategies they were never told about. | Single CTA to the consultation; set the expectation that Ray will name specific, dollar-quantified savings on the call. | Human, advisor-first close (reply goes to a real person) plus required results-vary / Circular 230 disclaimer.

**Summary:** Revamp (by JCE SEO, San Antonio) is a digital marketing agency that sells an integrated, outcome-based retainer it calls a 'Digital Revenue Engine' — combining SEO-optimized web design, local/national SEO, lead generation, PPC, and social media into one system. It serves owner-operated local and regional service businesses (HVAC, roofing, plumbing, law firms, med-spas, restaurants) who are invisible on Google and want predictable, measurable leads rather than commodity SEO. The entry point is a free Google Maps ranking assessment / SEO audit that leads into a strategy call and a monthly retainer.

**Rationale:** SEO has an unavoidable 60–90 day ramp, and the intake names 'slow results + no proactive communication' as the top churn risk. - Purpose: The hero objection-handler: name the cost-and-fit fear out loud, give enough pricing context to self-qualify, prove fit with named Boston-area client work, and offer a zero-risk free discovery call as the next step.
- Primary CTA: Book a free 20-minute discovery call
- Key points: Address the #1 hesitation head-on: every project is custom-quoted, and a quick call gives a clear, no-obligation number before you commit a dollar | Prove fit with real, relatable Boston work — logos and brand identity for small businesses like Boston Eyeworks, team branding for Youk's Kids, and event collateral for local nonprofits | Reframe the spend as credibility: clients end up hearing 'people keep asking who designed this' — design that makes them look legit | Low-friction close: a 20-minute discovery call, no pressure to buy, just a plan and a price
```

### Campaign 3: Discovery Call & Proposal Follow-Through
**Objective:** Maximize attended scoping calls and keep the deal moving by following every call with a same-day recap, scope, and proposal so warm inquiries don't go cold.  
**Rationale:** For a solo studio the scoping call is the revenue gate, but the moment that actually closes is the follow-up — sending the proposal while enthusiasm is fresh. Without it, a great conversation quietly stalls and the lead drifts away.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Sarah Carroll Design".

THIS EMAIL:

- Subject: Loved talking through your project — here's the recap + your proposal
- Preview/preheader: Everything we discussed, plus a simple next step to get started.
- Purpose: Same-day post-call recap that restates their goals, lays out the proposed scope, timeline to first concepts, and quote, then makes the kickoff step obvious — the single email that turns a conversation into a signed project.
- Primary CTA: Review your proposal & kick off
- Key points: Warm recap referencing their specific goals and the brand vision discussed on the call | Clear scope, timeline to the first concepts, and the custom quote — laid out with no surprises | One obvious next step to approve and kick off, with a note that the exciting part (first concepts) starts right after | Personal close inviting a reply with any questions — keep the momentum and the human touch

## Swift Financial Group, LLC
**URL:** https://swiftfinancialgroup.net  
**Vertical:** B2B/professional — financial services (seller-financed mortgage note buying)  
**Summary:** Swift Financial Group buys seller-financed (owner-financed) mortgage notes, converting a note holder's stream of future monthly payments into a single lump-sum cash payment at no cost to the seller. It serves individuals who financed a property sale themselves — retirees, small landlords, real estate investors, and heirs — who want immediate liquidity instead of waiting years to collect, including partial-note purchases for those who want some cash now and the note back later.

## United Against Fentanyl
**URL:** https://www.unitedagainstfentanyl.org  
**Vertical:** Education/Nonprofit/Advocacy  
**Summary:** United Against Fentanyl is a nonpartisan 501(c)(3) nonprofit fighting the fentanyl epidemic through peer grief support, national awareness events, education, and congressional advocacy. It serves families who have lost a loved one to fentanyl poisoning — primarily parents of 18-45-year-olds — along with concerned community members, offering a free network (the Fentanyl Families Network with weekly trauma-informed grief sessions), Walk for Lives events, and campaigns pressing Congress for bipartisan legislation. The organization is funded by donations and runs entirely on free, low-barrier participation.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Get a new newsletter or network signup to their first 'aha' moment — attending a weekly grief support session or finding a local Walk for Lives — within 7 days.  
**Rationale:** There is no automated welcome series today, yet the activation event — realizing you are not alone in a nationwide community — is fast, free, and self-serve. The fastest path to retention is getting a grieving newcomer into their first peer-led session before isolation pulls them away.

- Primary CTA: Reserve your seat at this week's session
- Key points: Acknowledge their loss or fear with empathy, without exploiting grief; affirm 'no other family should have to go through this' | Set expectations: free membership, weekly peer-led grief sessions, monthly crisis and policy updates — no barriers, no cost | Single first action: register for the next weekly trauma-informed session led by people with lived experience (not clinicians), so the first 'aha' lands within days | Point to a local Walk for Lives (July 11 multi-city; Sept 26 Washington DC) as an alternate entry point | Real human reply-to so a grieving newcomer can reach a person, not a no-reply address

## USOO
**URL:** https://usooapp.com  
**Vertical:** SaaS/tech — B2C consumer dating app (video speed dating, 18+)  
**Summary:** USOO is a video speed-dating app where singles join live, structured 5-minute face-to-face video calls with compatible matches, then independently Like or Pass — mutual likes unlock messaging, icebreaker games, and social chat rooms. It serves swipe-fatigued daters aged ~22–38 who want to feel real chemistry on camera before investing time in someone. The model is freemium (1 date/day free) converting to monthly Pro ($30) and Premium ($50) subscriptions.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding
**Objective:** Drive activation — get the new signup past video anxiety and into their first live 5-minute speed date, racing toward the 'It's a Match!' aha moment.  
**Rationale:** USOO is a novel format in beta — the single biggest risk is a signup who never joins a session because being on camera with a stranger feels scary. The welcome email has to convert curiosity into one brave click before the nerves win.  

**Email Prompt:**

```

- Subject: You're in. Your first 5 minutes could change everything.
- Preview/preheader: No swiping, no 'hey' that goes nowhere — just one real conversation.
- Purpose: Warm welcome, normalize the camera nerves in one line, and drive the single most important first action: join one live 5-minute date today.
- Primary CTA: Start my first speed date
- Key points: Reassure: it's only 5 minutes, both people opted in, and you can Pass with zero awkwardness — frame the nerves as the normal price of something real | Set the expectation that chemistry is felt fast on video, and the aha is the mutual match — most people get there within their first 1–3 sessions | One button, one action: join a live date now (free tier, 1/day); reply-to is a real human if they're nervous | Soft nudge to finish profile photo + bio first if missing, so they show up as their real self
```

- Campaign: Lapsed-Prospect Win-Back — Reactivate cold prospects — demo no-shows and audit downloaders who went quiet — and clean the list to protect deliverability.
- Subject: Still leaving money in your email list?
- Preview/preheader: Your list is probably still underperforming. Two minutes to change that.
- Purpose: Pattern-interrupt re-engagement that reminds the lapsed prospect of the core value and gives one low-friction reason to come back.
- Primary CTA: See what your list could earn
- Key points: Acknowledge the gap without guilt — 'we never finished the conversation' | Restate the core value: more inbox placement, more revenue, none of the in-house lift | Offer a fresh, lower-commitment entry point (re-run the free audit or grab a short call) | Single clear CTA; non-responders route to a final sunset email before suppression
```
