## Zippy Entertainment
**URL:** https://www.zippyisfunny.com  
**Vertical:** Local & service (mobile event entertainment)  
**Summary:** Zippy Entertainment is a Phoenix-metro mobile event-entertainment company that brings foam, bubble, and gender-reveal parties, balloon artistry, face painting, character appearances, and magic shows directly to a client's event location. It serves parents (ages 25-45) planning kids' birthdays and family celebrations, plus corporate, school, and community clients, on a one-off per-event booking secured by a 50% non-refundable retainer.  

### Campaign 1: Welcome & Onboarding (Post-Booking Confirmation)
**Objective:** Confirm the booking instantly, manufacture an early 'aha' by reassuring the host they chose right, and set expectations so the event runs flawlessly.  
**Rationale:** Everything is greenfield and a confirmed booking is Zippy's highest-trust moment — a professional confirmation is the pre-event 'aha' that calms reliability anxiety, locks in excitement, and reduces last-minute cancellations on a non-refundable retainer.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Zippy Entertainment".

Brand colors: primary #1BAEEA, accent #FF4500, background #FFFFFF, text #1A1A2E.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Welcome & Onboarding (Post-Booking Confirmation) — Confirm the booking instantly, manufacture an early 'aha' by reassuring the host they chose right, and set expectations so the event runs flawlessly.
- Subject: 🎉 You're officially booked — foam day is locked in!
- Preview/preheader: Your date's secured. Here's what happens next (and the one thing we'll need from you).
- Purpose: Instantly confirm the date is locked, reassure the host they picked a licensed/insured/guaranteed pro, and tell them exactly what happens next.
- Primary CTA: Add your event to your calendar
- Key points: Confirm the exact date, time, service, and location back to them so they know it's real and correct | Reassure: licensed, insured, bonded, FBI-cleared, and backed by the 100% satisfaction guarantee — they chose right | Set expectations: Zippy handles all setup, operation, and cleanup — zero effort for the host | Preview the prep checklist coming closer to the date (water hookup, clear space) so there are no surprises | Warm, real reply-to invite: 'Have a question before the big day? Just hit reply.'
```

### Campaign 2: Inquiry-to-Booking Conversion
**Objective:** Turn an availability-check / contact-form submission into a paid 50% retainer by confirming the date is open, answering the price objection, and creating calendar urgency.  
**Rationale:** The brand's #1 goal this quarter is converting inquiries into bookings, and right now non-converting form submissions get zero follow-up — this is lost revenue sitting idle, and the top objection (price) plus availability fear are both fixable in one well-timed send.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Zippy Entertainment".

Brand colors: primary #1BAEEA, accent #FF4500, background #FFFFFF, text #1A1A2E.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Inquiry-to-Booking Conversion — Turn an availability-check / contact-form submission into a paid 50% retainer by confirming the date is open, answering the price objection, and creating calendar urgency.
- Subject: Good news — your date is still open! 🙌
- Preview/preheader: Here's your quote, what's included, and how to lock it in before someone grabs the slot.
- Purpose: Confirm availability for their date, deliver the quote, justify the premium with proof, and make locking the date one easy step.
- Primary CTA: Lock in my date with a 50% retainer
- Key points: Lead with the relief: 'Yes, [event date] is available!' — kills the availability objection immediately | Reframe price as value: a stress-free, mind-blowing experience the kids will talk about for months vs. a DIY headache or a bounce-house rental | Stack the proof: video testimonials, photo gallery, and the 100% satisfaction guarantee (free event up to 15 guests if Zippy ever misses a confirmed booking) | Create real urgency: popular Phoenix-metro dates book 4-6 weeks to a year out — a 50% retainer (Venmo/Zelle) holds the date now | Offer a quick call/reply for any questions on package options or add-ons
```

### Campaign 3: Booking Reminders & Event-Day Prep
**Objective:** Make sure the event goes off without a hitch and prevent last-minute cancellations by delivering logistics prep and building excitement as the date approaches.  
**Rationale:** This is a logistics-heavy live service where a missed water hookup or unclear space can wreck the experience — reminders cut no-shows ~35% and the prep checklist turns a nervous host into a prepared, hyped one, protecting the event and the review that follows.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Zippy Entertainment".

Brand colors: primary #1BAEEA, accent #FF4500, background #FFFFFF, text #1A1A2E.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Booking Reminders & Event-Day Prep — Make sure the event goes off without a hitch and prevent last-minute cancellations by delivering logistics prep and building excitement as the date approaches.
- Subject: 2 days till foam day! 🫧 Your quick prep checklist
- Preview/preheader: A garden hose, a clear space, and excited kids — that's all we need from you.
- Purpose: The make-or-break prep email: give the host the short logistics checklist and final what-to-expect so setup is flawless, while ramping excitement.
- Primary CTA: Review your day-of checklist
- Key points: Countdown excitement: 'The kids have no idea what's about to hit them — in the best way!' | Simple host checklist: accessible water spigot/garden hose, a clear flat area of the right size, and a power outlet if needed | What to expect on the day: arrival/setup window, run-of-show, and that Zippy handles all teardown and cleanup | Confirm the locked details (date, time, address) and include the reschedule/contact link to remove any friction | Reminder of the guarantee + a direct phone/reply line for any last-minute questions
```

### Campaign 4: Anniversary & Renewal (Annual Re-Booking)
**Objective:** Drive repeat bookings by reaching past clients before the next annual celebration and prompting them to lock the date again — ideally with an upgrade.  
**Rationale:** Birthdays recur every year and corporate clients book annually, but one-and-done customers don't realize they can rebook — a timed anniversary nudge captures the highest-intent repeat moment Zippy has and beats price-shopping competitors to the calendar slot.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Zippy Entertainment".

Brand colors: primary #1BAEEA, accent #FF4500, background #FFFFFF, text #1A1A2E.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Anniversary & Renewal (Annual Re-Booking) — Drive repeat bookings by reaching past clients before the next annual celebration and prompting them to lock the date again — ideally with an upgrade.
- Subject: Can you believe it's almost party time again?! 🎂
- Preview/preheader: Last year's foam party was epic — let's lock this year's date before it books up.
- Purpose: Trigger the rebooking with nostalgia from last year's event plus early-bird urgency to secure the date before it fills.
- Primary CTA: Check availability for this year
- Key points: Lead with the memory: 'About a year ago we turned your yard into a foam wonderland — and we'd love to do it again!' | Make rebooking effortless: 'Reply with your date and we'll check availability today' | Early-bird urgency: popular dates book months out — secure it now to avoid the last-minute scramble | Soft expansion nudge: add Glow-in-the-Dark foam, a balloon arch, face painting, or a character appearance to level up this year | Returning-client appreciation: mention the repeat/extended-booking discount as a thank-you for coming back
```

### Campaign 5: Post-Event Review & Referral
**Objective:** Capture a review and photos while the joy is fresh, and turn delighted hosts into a referral channel.  
**Rationale:** Zippy already runs on word-of-mouth but has zero structured way to capture or amplify it — asking right after the 'wow moment' converts genuine delight into reviews, shareable photos, and warm referrals that feed the top of the funnel for free.  

**Email Prompt:**

```
Generate ONE responsive HTML marketing email for the brand "Zippy Entertainment".

Brand colors: primary #1BAEEA, accent #FF4500, background #FFFFFF, text #1A1A2E.

THIS EMAIL:
- Campaign: Post-Event Review & Referral — Capture a review and photos while the joy is fresh, and turn delighted hosts into a referral channel.
- Subject: Did the kids have a blast?? 🎉 (one quick favor)
- Preview/preheader: Share the photos, leave a quick review — and grab a thank-you for your next party.
- Purpose: Ride the post-party high to request a review, prompt a photo share, and plant the referral ask with a clear reward for both sides.
- Primary CTA: Leave a 30-second review
- Key points: Open with shared joy: 'Those first 5 minutes when the foam hit — pure magic, right?' | Single primary ask: a quick Google review with a direct link (lowest-friction advocacy) | Photo-share prompt: 'Got pics or video? Tag us — we love reliving the chaos' | Referral offer framed for both sides: a perk for them and a treat for the friend they send Zippy's way | Warm close reminding them rebooking is easy whenever the next celebration comes around
```
